< text>
I rate this outfit ZERO (on a scale of 0 to 10) for customer service. I was there today at around 5 PM (BTW, I was the only customer in the store) for

1) unlocking an iphone that I bought from Sprint and has long been paid for;

2) activating a phone using one of the Sprint SIM cards that I never used (I had 5 lines when I first signed up the Sprint service 3 years ago but I only used 3 of the lines at that time, so there were 2 unused SIM cards in my possession)

There were three of the sales/customer support type in the store; one of them greeted me. Upon hearing what I was there for, she started saying "you should ask your new carrier to unlock the phone for you because they are making money off you;" when I asked her to activate my phone, she said we are T-Mobile not Sprint, can't activate Sprint SIM card. Then I told her, I had talked to the T-Mobile customer support rep on the phone and was advised to go to a T-Mobile store for phone activation, she said it's easy for them to offload the work on us. At this juncture, the woman sitting behind the counter chimed in, "we only do sales here, nothing else." And the guy behind the counter said, "you have to call Sprint to get help."

I left their store and went straight to the T-Mobile shop in the Westfield Mall where the lady at the counter was very helpful, she swapped my 2 Sprint SIM cards for the new T-Mobile SIM cards, activated one of my phones, helped me call T-Mobile to get my phone unlocked -- all free of charge!

Don't ever come to this store for anything 'cause you will get zip, zilch, nada, ZERO services from these no good, lazy, lowlifes (BTW, they hardly speak English); if you live in the area, go to the T-Mobile stores in Westfield Mall, and yes, there are two T-Mobile stores there.</text>

This is a new restaurant that took over the old Baja Fresh. The restaurant is a nice little family run place with tables and sushi bar. Sadly, the new restaurant cannot get away from the sewer gas smell that comes out of the drains - and has for years. I don't know how they can solve a design flaw...

<Review>Always spicey at Chandara! Got met with a little apprehension walking thru the door with 9 people and no reservations but as dinner got underway our presence was more warmly welcomed.
No "birthday desserts" we were told. Ordered fried banana with Coconut ice cream, not bad :)
Order light as entre portions are large, and spices are Thai spicey not American.
Ordered drunken noodles last time, spicey. They were almost to much... almost.
Father in-law got regular and said they were HOT! Very quiet the 3 times I have been here and there always seems to be a good bit of room for seating. Relatively new restaurant in town (September 2018) still seems to be finding its footing but the food is VERY solid and I will be back.</Review>< UserId.>

This was not only the worst thai food I have ever had,  it was the worst food I have ever ordered from a restaurant in my entire life. My food was over salted to the point of being inedible and had none of the characteristics of the very common Thai dish I ordered other than it contained beef. The water was also very bad. It was either very heavily chlorinated or both of the glasses at my table had large amounts of dish detergent residue. I recommend drinking beer instead,  as it will come in a bottle and remove Chandara from the entire equation. You will also appreciate the alcohol as your outing at this awful restaurant continues.

My server wasn't nearly as terrible as my food was, but how the restaurant responded when I sent my food back was awkward, unprofessional, rude and brief.

In short, I cannot recommend Chandara in any way. It wasn't just bad Thai food like panda express is bad Chinese food, it was bad food in general. Chandara should immediately clean house and get new cooks, and possibly a new dishwasher.

-edit-
I thought I should mention that I have never posted a review on Google before, but my experience at Chandara was so terrible I decided I should warn everybody. Nobody deserves 5 top ramen flavor packets masquerading as thai food.<//text>
